- Log -----------------------------------------------------------------
commit a8eba56ef62af2f9a5b46825c994665cd3789c2e
Author: Dr. Stephen Henson <steve at openssl.org>
Date:   Thu Jan 7 17:02:20 2016 +0000

    use more descriptive name DEFINE_STACK_OF_CONST
    
    Reviewed-by: Richard Levitte <levitte at openssl.org>

commit 4a1f3f274108e25b97bd9870170fe2970892e155
Author: Dr. Stephen Henson <steve at openssl.org>
Date:   Wed Jan 6 02:54:18 2016 +0000

    Only declare stacks in headers
    
    Don't define stacks in C source files: it causes warnings
    about unused functions in some compilers.
    
    Reviewed-by: Richard Levitte <levitte at openssl.org>

commit 858857157290dd35145b14044ae96be9cd8eb0df
Author: Dr. Stephen Henson <steve at openssl.org>
Date:   Mon Dec 28 00:04:33 2015 +0000

    Rename DECLARE*STACK_OF to DEFINE*STACK_OF
    
    Applications wishing to include their own stacks now just need to include
    
    DEFINE_STACK_OF(foo)
    
    in a header file.
    
    Reviewed-by: Richard Levitte <levitte at openssl.org>

commit c5e0c5404708939a3bed317366367d9898960598
Author: Dr. Stephen Henson <steve at openssl.org>
Date:   Sun Dec 27 23:46:39 2015 +0000

    remove unused PREDECLARE
    
    Reviewed-by: Richard Levitte <levitte at openssl.org>

commit 4a640fb6c395302d7aad22833d573c44211b0a2d
Author: Dr. Stephen Henson <steve at openssl.org>
Date:   Wed Dec 23 00:47:28 2015 +0000

    Fix declarations and constification for inline stack.
    
    Reviewed-by: Richard Levitte <levitte at openssl.org>

commit 411abf2dd37974a5baa54859c1abcd287b3c1181
Author: Dr. Stephen Henson <steve at openssl.org>
Date:   Wed Dec 23 00:47:13 2015 +0000

    Change STACK_OF to use inline functions.
    
    Change DECLARE_STACK_OF into inline functions. This avoids the need for
    auto generated mkstack.pl macros and now handles const properly.
    
    Reviewed-by: Richard Levitte <levitte at openssl.org>
